> **SomeGuyDude said:**
> Same menubar, same tabs, the Metacity themes are very close, both have that idea of a colored band at the top, the buttons aren't TOO different. Some minor shape differences and ClearGlow's menu bar is a little fatter. A few other minor differences, but switching between the two almost feels like they're slight mods of the same core idea.

I don't know which came first, so I'm not accusing anyone of copying the other.

I don't think they're all that similar. I just tried Clearglow, and while it shares the overall concept, the execution and intended audience is clearly different. The author even mentioned the influence by Shiki & others in the webpage, so assuming any influences are open source, there shouldn't be a problem. Besides, there have been many themes before Shiki and CG that used similar arrangements, it just happens that these new sets of themes coming out recently are the most refined/perfected forms of this style yet.

It's better to have more choices, and the prevalence of the design can only help improve it. For example, the author of CG helped me fix an xfce bug in Shiki, so things like that happen and are good for everyone.

### Post by What is in a name? on 2008-08-30
> **Mark76 said:**
> Why is it called "Elegant Brit"?

Back then, after observing Elegant One, I thought that perhaps I could do something pretty if I made a theme based in blue and red. Probably the oldest widget of all in that first vision I had was the lower-right corner's handle which is used to resize the window. That little triangular shape was sort of inspired by the design that appeared on the tail of the old British Airways planes. It guided all the rest of the theme.

[IMG]http://news.bbc.co.uk/olmedia/350000/images/_351402_ba_tails_300.jpg[/IMG]

In the end, instead of using pure red, which would be too strong to be presented on the screen (and if I darkened that red colour, it probably would look dull side by side with the dark blue pixmaps), I decided to find a sort of a red-orange tone. It pleased me and some other people. Others considered the orange tone was TOO orange and bright for their eyes.

In other words, surprisingly enough, Elegant Brit owes a lot of its concept to... A flag! I always had this slight emotional connection to Britain, the English language (especially the British variant, which is why many times I prefer to say "colour" instead of "color", etc.), some of the institutions, and many other aspects of the British culture, since my mother was born in Bermuda and therefore I grew up in a bi-cultural (perhaps tri-cultural, considering the Bermudians feel and are closer to the USA) and also bilingual home.

The name, "Elegant Brit", besides its obvious connection to Elegant One, ended up having a double meaning. Politeness, civility and perhaps some over the board pride are some of the qualities people traditionally associate with the Brits (at least the 19th century ones with bowler hats and canes, hehehe). I wanted to make sure my first theme ever was also tasteful, clean and pleasant, even if minimalistic. I didn't want to make it look outdated, though. LOL. After all, London is one of the most cosmopolitan and modern cities in the world, right?

Disclaimer: the above has no particular influence on my political views, nor am I a defender of the "empire" or whatever people might want to call it. Being Portuguese is enough to teach me about the dangers of megalomania. I could use some of that Northern cold blood, tho. 

Finally, I'm obviously somewhat thrilled about London's Olympic Games in 2012. Ha.

---

### Post by OrangeCrate on 2008-08-30

---

### Post by What is in a name? on 2008-08-30
> **OrangeCrate said:**
> Yes, that's what I attempted to do.

What I said, is that the new icon is not listed in the available pixmap options. I can even change the Xfce main menu icon to a Gnome icon (LOL), but not the one that comes with the new theme. It's simply not there, and if it's hiding somewhere else, I don't know how to find it.

Thanks for the response, I appreciate it.

Well, use that same file browsing dialog to go to your home folder, and then to your .icons folder, where your newly installed icon themes should be. When inside of your preferred icon theme, pick the size you prefer and then open the "places" folder. There you'll find a start-here.png icon (or start-here.svg, if you're inside of the "scalable" folder).

---

### Post by Mr.Crowley on 2008-08-31
> **Patricrawley said:**
> Daft Punk ftw! I already saved the background from your other reply, but do you have any other backgrounds like this, in a similar style or do you know where to get it? Because it is most danq, my friend.
If you like that style I suggest looking into vector graphics/art. Peruse deviart under 'digital art --> vector' or 'customization --> wallpaper --> vector' and you will see alot like it. Also, check out _[j3concepts]("http://www.jthreeconcepts.com/work.html")_. Hope that helps. In the meantime, _[here]("http://www.mediafire.com/?dymxmnan0jd")_ is the same background in a different color; three different resolutions.
